Vollkorn Regular (Vollkorn[wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Vollkorn-Regular', Everything looks good.

This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software. The result of sTypoAscender – sTypoDescender should match or exceed the unitsPerEm value.

The result of sTypoAscender – sTypoDescender (1393) match or exceed the unitsPerEm value (1000).

gasp Table

gasp Table

Pass

Vollkorn Regular (Vollkorn[wght].ttf)

gasp

Version

gasp table verison should be 1.

Verison = 1

Info

Vollkorn Regular (Vollkorn[wght].ttf)

gasp

Default

Pull gasp table Default.

Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True

Pass

Vollkorn Regular (Vollkorn[wght].ttf)

gasp

Default

Check gasp table Default.

gasp table default is:
Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True
and should be:
Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True

PostScript names

PostScript names

Pass

Vollkorn Regular (Vollkorn[wght].ttf)

post

PostScript names

Postscript names should not be longer then 29 characters. May cause issues in PDF.

Every PostScript name is fine.

Pass

Vollkorn Italic (Vollkorn-Italic[wght].ttf)

post

PostScript names

Postscript names should not be longer then 29 characters. May cause issues in PDF.

Every PostScript name is fine.

GSUB

sinf

If there is a feature subs, then the sinf feature should be there, too. Otherwise InDesign will mark it not existing.

There is a subs feature in the font, but the sinf is missing. Please investigate.
